[2019/09/20 03:10:13] SQL Query: SELECT c.CODIGO, c.NOMBRE, activos.activo, pasivos.pasivo, capitales.capital
      FROM dp01a110 c 
      LEFT JOIN 
        (SELECT CODMOV, ID_EMPRESA, SUM(IMPORTE) AS activo
         FROM dpmovimi 
         WHERE FECHA_ASI <= '2018-08-02' AND ( CODMOV LIKE '1%' ) AND ID_EMPRESA = 4 GROUP BY CODMOV) AS activos ON activos.CODMOV = c.CODIGO
        LEFT JOIN
          (SELECT CODMOV, ID_EMPRESA, SUM(IMPORTE) AS pasivo
           FROM dpmovimi 
           WHERE FECHA_ASI <= '2018-08-02' AND (  CODMOV LIKE '2%'  ) AND ID_EMPRESA = 4 GROUP BY CODMOV) AS pasivos ON pasivos.CODMOV = c.CODIGO
      LEFT JOIN
          (SELECT CODMOV, ID_EMPRESA, SUM(IMPORTE) AS capital
           FROM dpmovimi 
           WHERE FECHA_ASI <= '2018-08-02' AND (  CODMOV LIKE '3%'  ) AND ID_EMPRESA = 4 GROUP BY CODMOV) AS capitales ON capitales.CODMOV = c.CODIGO
        WHERE (c.CTAINACTIVA IS NULL OR c.CTAINACTIVA = 0) AND (  c.CODIGO LIKE '1%' OR c.CODIGO LIKE '2%' OR c.CODIGO LIKE '3%'  ) ORDER BY c.CODIGO, activos.activo, capitales.capital;

[2019/09/20 03:43:41] SQL Query: SELECT CODIGO,NOMBRE FROM dp01a110 WHERE CODIGO_AUX = '38'
[2019/09/20 03:43:41] SQL Query: SELECT c.CODIGO, c.NOMBRE, activos.activo, pasivos.pasivo, capitales.capital
      FROM dp01a110 c 
      LEFT JOIN 
        (SELECT CODMOV, ID_EMPRESA, SUM(IMPORTE) AS activo
         FROM dpmovimi 
         WHERE FECHA_ASI <= '2018-08-01' AND ( CODMOV LIKE '1%' ) AND ID_EMPRESA = 4 GROUP BY CODMOV) AS activos ON activos.CODMOV = c.CODIGO
        LEFT JOIN
          (SELECT CODMOV, ID_EMPRESA, SUM(IMPORTE) AS pasivo
           FROM dpmovimi 
           WHERE FECHA_ASI <= '2018-08-01' AND (  CODMOV LIKE '2%'  ) AND ID_EMPRESA = 4 GROUP BY CODMOV) AS pasivos ON pasivos.CODMOV = c.CODIGO
      LEFT JOIN
          (SELECT CODMOV, ID_EMPRESA, SUM(IMPORTE) AS capital
           FROM dpmovimi 
           WHERE FECHA_ASI <= '2018-08-01' AND (  CODMOV LIKE '3%'  ) AND ID_EMPRESA = 4 GROUP BY CODMOV) AS capitales ON capitales.CODMOV = c.CODIGO
        WHERE (c.CTAINACTIVA IS NULL OR c.CTAINACTIVA = 0) AND (  c.CODIGO LIKE '1%' OR c.CODIGO LIKE '2%' OR c.CODIGO LIKE '3%'  ) ORDER BY c.CODIGO, activos.activo, capitales.capital;

[2019/09/20 03:45:12] SQL Query: SELECT c.CODIGO, c.NOMBRE, activos.activo, pasivos.pasivo, capitales.capital
      FROM dp01a110 c 
      LEFT JOIN 
        (SELECT CODMOV, ID_EMPRESA, SUM(IMPORTE) AS activo
         FROM dpmovimi 
         WHERE FECHA_ASI <= '2018-08-01' AND ( CODMOV LIKE '1%' ) AND ID_EMPRESA = 4 GROUP BY CODMOV) AS activos ON activos.CODMOV = c.CODIGO
        LEFT JOIN
          (SELECT CODMOV, ID_EMPRESA, SUM(IMPORTE) AS pasivo
           FROM dpmovimi 
           WHERE FECHA_ASI <= '2018-08-01' AND (  CODMOV LIKE '2%'  ) AND ID_EMPRESA = 4 GROUP BY CODMOV) AS pasivos ON pasivos.CODMOV = c.CODIGO
      LEFT JOIN
          (SELECT CODMOV, ID_EMPRESA, SUM(IMPORTE) AS capital
           FROM dpmovimi 
           WHERE FECHA_ASI <= '2018-08-01' AND (  CODMOV LIKE '3%'  ) AND ID_EMPRESA = 4 GROUP BY CODMOV) AS capitales ON capitales.CODMOV = c.CODIGO
        WHERE (c.CTAINACTIVA IS NULL OR c.CTAINACTIVA = 0) AND (  c.CODIGO LIKE '1%' OR c.CODIGO LIKE '2%' OR c.CODIGO LIKE '3%'  ) ORDER BY c.CODIGO, activos.activo, capitales.capital;

[2019/09/20 03:47:34] SQL Query: SELECT c.CODIGO, c.NOMBRE, activos.activo, pasivos.pasivo, capitales.capital
      FROM dp01a110 c 
      LEFT JOIN 
        (SELECT CODMOV, ID_EMPRESA, SUM(IMPORTE) AS activo
         FROM dpmovimi 
         WHERE FECHA_ASI <= '2018-08-01' AND ( CODMOV LIKE '1%' ) AND ID_EMPRESA = 4 GROUP BY CODMOV) AS activos ON activos.CODMOV = c.CODIGO
        LEFT JOIN
          (SELECT CODMOV, ID_EMPRESA, SUM(IMPORTE) AS pasivo
           FROM dpmovimi 
           WHERE FECHA_ASI <= '2018-08-01' AND (  CODMOV LIKE '2%'  ) AND ID_EMPRESA = 4 GROUP BY CODMOV) AS pasivos ON pasivos.CODMOV = c.CODIGO
      LEFT JOIN
          (SELECT CODMOV, ID_EMPRESA, SUM(IMPORTE) AS capital
           FROM dpmovimi 
           WHERE FECHA_ASI <= '2018-08-01' AND (  CODMOV LIKE '3%'  ) AND ID_EMPRESA = 4 GROUP BY CODMOV) AS capitales ON capitales.CODMOV = c.CODIGO
        WHERE (c.CTAINACTIVA IS NULL OR c.CTAINACTIVA = 0) AND (  c.CODIGO LIKE '1%' OR c.CODIGO LIKE '2%' OR c.CODIGO LIKE '3%'  ) ORDER BY c.CODIGO, activos.activo, capitales.capital;

[2019/09/20 04:26:26] SQL Query: SELECT c.CODIGO, c.NOMBRE, activos.activo, pasivos.pasivo, capitales.capital
      FROM dp01a110 c 
      LEFT JOIN 
        (SELECT CODMOV, ID_EMPRESA, SUM(IMPORTE) AS activo
         FROM dpmovimi 
         WHERE FECHA_ASI <= '2018-08-31' AND ( CODMOV LIKE '1%' ) AND ID_EMPRESA = 4 GROUP BY CODMOV) AS activos ON activos.CODMOV = c.CODIGO
        LEFT JOIN
          (SELECT CODMOV, ID_EMPRESA, SUM(IMPORTE) AS pasivo
           FROM dpmovimi 
           WHERE FECHA_ASI <= '2018-08-31' AND (  CODMOV LIKE '2%'  ) AND ID_EMPRESA = 4 GROUP BY CODMOV) AS pasivos ON pasivos.CODMOV = c.CODIGO
            LEFT JOIN
            (SELECT CODMOV, ID_EMPRESA, SUM(IMPORTE) AS capital
            FROM dpmovimi 
            WHERE FECHA_ASI <= '2018-08-31' AND (  CODMOV LIKE '3%'  ) AND ID_EMPRESA = 4 GROUP BY CODMOV) AS capitales ON capitales.CODMOV = c.CODIGO
            WHERE (c.CTAINACTIVA IS NULL OR c.CTAINACTIVA = 0) AND (  c.CODIGO LIKE '1%' OR c.CODIGO LIKE '2%' OR c.CODIGO LIKE '3%'  ) ORDER BY c.CODIGO, activos.activo, capitales.capital;

         FROM dpmovimi

          (SELECT CODMOV, ID_EMPRESA, SUM(IMPORTE) AS pasivo
           FROM dpmovimi

[2019/09/23 08:25:38] SQL Query: SELECT CODIGO,NOMBRE FROM dp01a110 WHERE CODIGO_AUX = '38'
[2019/09/23 08:25:38] SQL Query: SELECT c.CODIGO, c.NOMBRE, activos.activo, pasivos.pasivo, capitales.capital
      FROM dp01a110 c 
      LEFT JOIN 
        (SELECT CODMOV, ID_EMPRESA, SUM(IMPORTE) AS activo
         FROM dpmovimi 
         WHERE FECHA_ASI <= '2018-08-01' AND ( CODMOV LIKE '1%' ) AND ID_EMPRESA = 4 GROUP BY CODMOV) AS activos ON activos.CODMOV = c.CODIGO
        LEFT JOIN
          (SELECT CODMOV, ID_EMPRESA, SUM(IMPORTE) AS pasivo
           FROM dpmovimi 
           WHERE FECHA_ASI <= '2018-08-01' AND (  CODMOV LIKE '2%'  ) AND ID_EMPRESA = 4 GROUP BY CODMOV) AS pasivos ON pasivos.CODMOV = c.CODIGO
            LEFT JOIN
            (SELECT CODMOV, ID_EMPRESA, SUM(IMPORTE) AS capital
            FROM dpmovimi 
            WHERE FECHA_ASI <= '2018-08-01' AND (  CODMOV LIKE '3%'  ) AND ID_EMPRESA = 4 GROUP BY CODMOV) AS capitales ON capitales.CODMOV = c.CODIGO
            WHERE (c.CTAINACTIVA IS NULL OR c.CTAINACTIVA = 0) AND (  c.CODIGO LIKE '1%' OR c.CODIGO LIKE '2%' OR c.CODIGO LIKE '3%'  ) ORDER BY c.CODIGO, activos.activo, capitales.capital;

[2019/09/23 08:30:40] SQL Query: SELECT CODIGO,NOMBRE FROM dp01a110 WHERE CODIGO_AUX = '38'
[2019/09/23 08:30:40] SQL Query: SELECT c.CODIGO, c.NOMBRE, activos.activo, pasivos.pasivo, capitales.capital
      FROM dp01a110 c 
      LEFT JOIN 
        (SELECT CODMOV, ID_EMPRESA, SUM(IMPORTE) AS activo
         FROM dpmovimi 
         WHERE FECHA_ASI <= '2018-08-01' AND ( CODMOV LIKE '1%' ) AND ID_EMPRESA = 4 GROUP BY CODMOV) AS activos ON activos.CODMOV = c.CODIGO
        LEFT JOIN
          (SELECT CODMOV, ID_EMPRESA, SUM(IMPORTE) AS pasivo
           FROM dpmovimi 
           WHERE FECHA_ASI <= '2018-08-01' AND (  CODMOV LIKE '2%'  ) AND ID_EMPRESA = 4 GROUP BY CODMOV) AS pasivos ON pasivos.CODMOV = c.CODIGO
            LEFT JOIN
            (SELECT CODMOV, ID_EMPRESA, SUM(IMPORTE) AS capital
            FROM dpmovimi 
            WHERE FECHA_ASI <= '2018-08-01' AND (  CODMOV LIKE '3%'  ) AND ID_EMPRESA = 4 GROUP BY CODMOV) AS capitales ON capitales.CODMOV = c.CODIGO
            WHERE (c.CTAINACTIVA IS NULL OR c.CTAINACTIVA = 0) AND (  c.CODIGO LIKE '1%' OR c.CODIGO LIKE '2%' OR c.CODIGO LIKE '3%'  ) ORDER BY c.CODIGO, activos.activo, capitales.capital;

[2019/09/23 08:35:42] SQL Query: SELECT CODIGO,NOMBRE FROM dp01a110 WHERE CODIGO_AUX = '38'
[2019/09/23 08:35:42] SQL Query: SELECT c.CODIGO, c.NOMBRE, activos.activo, pasivos.pasivo, capitales.capital
      FROM dp01a110 c 
      LEFT JOIN 
        (SELECT CODMOV, ID_EMPRESA, SUM(IMPORTE) AS activo
         FROM dpmovimi 
         WHERE FECHA_ASI <= '2018-08-01' AND ( CODMOV LIKE '1%' ) AND ID_EMPRESA = 4 GROUP BY CODMOV) AS activos ON activos.CODMOV = c.CODIGO
        LEFT JOIN
          (SELECT CODMOV, ID_EMPRESA, SUM(IMPORTE) AS pasivo
           FROM dpmovimi 
           WHERE FECHA_ASI <= '2018-08-01' AND (  CODMOV LIKE '2%'  ) AND ID_EMPRESA = 4 GROUP BY CODMOV) AS pasivos ON pasivos.CODMOV = c.CODIGO
            LEFT JOIN
            (SELECT CODMOV, ID_EMPRESA, SUM(IMPORTE) AS capital
            FROM dpmovimi 
            WHERE FECHA_ASI <= '2018-08-01' AND (  CODMOV LIKE '3%'  ) AND ID_EMPRESA = 4 GROUP BY CODMOV) AS capitales ON capitales.CODMOV = c.CODIGO
            WHERE (c.CTAINACTIVA IS NULL OR c.CTAINACTIVA = 0) AND (  c.CODIGO LIKE '1%' OR c.CODIGO LIKE '2%' OR c.CODIGO LIKE '3%'  ) ORDER BY c.CODIGO, activos.activo, capitales.capital;

      FROM dp01a110 c 
      LEFT JOIN 
        (SELECT CODMOV, ID_EMPRESA, SUM(IMPORTE) AS activo
         FROM dpmovimi 
         WHERE FECHA_ASI <= '2018-08-01' AND ( CODMOV LIKE '1%' ) AND ID_EMPRESA = 4 GROUP BY CODMOV) AS activos ON activos.CODMOV = c.CODIGO
        LEFT JOIN
          (SELECT CODMOV, ID_EMPRESA, SUM(IMPORTE) AS pasivo
           FROM dpmovimi 
           WHERE FECHA_ASI <= '2018-08-01' AND (  CODMOV LIKE '2%'  ) AND ID_EMPRESA = 4 GROUP BY CODMOV) AS pasivos ON pasivos.CODMOV = c.CODIGO
            LEFT JOIN

            FROM dpmovimi 
            WHERE FECHA_ASI <= '2018-08-01' AND (  CODMOV LIKE '3%'  ) AND ID_EMPRESA = 4 GROUP BY CODMOV) AS capitales ON capitales.CODMOV = c.CODIGO

      FROM dp01a110 c 
      LEFT JOIN 
        (SELECT CODMOV, ID_EMPRESA, SUM(IMPORTE) AS activo
         FROM dpmovimi 
         WHERE FECHA_ASI <= '2018-08-01' AND ( CODMOV LIKE '1%' ) AND ID_EMPRESA = 4 GROUP BY CODMOV) AS activos ON activos.CODMOV = c.CODIGO
        LEFT JOIN
          (SELECT CODMOV, ID_EMPRESA, SUM(IMPORTE) AS pasivo
           FROM dpmovimi 
           WHERE FECHA_ASI <= '2018-08-01' AND (  CODMOV LIKE '2%'  ) AND ID_EMPRESA = 4 GROUP BY CODMOV) AS pasivos ON pasivos.CODMOV = c.CODIGO
            LEFT JOIN

      FROM dp01a110 c

         FROM dpmovimi 
         WHERE FECHA_ASI <= '2018-08-01' AND ( CODMOV LIKE '1%' ) AND ID_EMPRESA = 4 GROUP BY CODMOV) AS activos ON activos.CODMOV = c.CODIGO
        LEFT JOIN
          (SELECT CODMOV, ID_EMPRESA, SUM(IMPORTE) AS pasivo
           FROM dpmovimi 
           WHERE FECHA_ASI <= '2018-08-01' AND (  CODMOV LIKE '2%'  ) AND ID_EMPRESA = 4 GROUP BY CODMOV) AS pasivos ON pasivos.CODMOV = c.CODIGO

      FROM dp01a110 c

         FROM dpmovimi 
         WHERE FECHA_ASI <= '2018-08-01' AND ( CODMOV LIKE '1%' ) AND ID_EMPRESA = 4 GROUP BY CODMOV) AS activos ON activos.CODMOV = c.CODIGO

          (SELECT CODMOV, ID_EMPRESA, SUM(IMPORTE) AS pasivo
           FROM dpmovimi

         FROM dpmovimi

          (SELECT CODMOV, ID_EMPRESA, SUM(IMPORTE) AS pasivo
           FROM dpmovimi
